color: rgb(47, 111, 159);"><span style="background-color: transparent;"><span style="font-size: inherit;">&gt;</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></div><code style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: inherit; padding: 0px 45px 0px 0px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); border-radius: 0px; display: inline-block; background-color: transparent;">    Dropdown<br/>
    <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;span</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">class=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;caret&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;&lt;/span&gt;</span><br/>
  <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;/button&gt;</span><br/>
  <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;ul</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">class=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;dropdown-menu&quot;</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">aria-labelledby=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;dropdownMenu1&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span><br/>
    <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;li&gt;&lt;a</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">href=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;#&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span>Action<span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</span><br/>
    <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;li&gt;&lt;a</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">href=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;#&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span>Another action<span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</span><br/>
    <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;li&gt;&lt;a</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">href=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;#&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span>Something else here<span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</span><br/>
    <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;li&gt;&lt;a</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">href=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;#&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span>Separated link<span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</span></code><div><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><span style="font-size: 13px;"><span style="font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace;"><span style="font-size: inherit;"><span style="background-color: transparent;"> </span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);"><span style="background-color: transparent;"><span style="font-size: inherit;">&lt;/ul&gt;</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></div><div><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><span style="font-size: 13px;"><span style="font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace;"><span style="font-size: inherit;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);"><span style="background-color: transparent;"><span style="font-size: inherit;">&lt;/div&gt;</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></div><div><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><span style="font-size: 13px;"><span style="font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace;"><span style="color: rgb(47, 111, 159);"><br/></span></span></span></span></div><div><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; display: inline !important; float: none; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">通过为下拉菜单的父元素设置 </span><code style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace; font-size: 14.4px; padding: 2px 4px; color: rgb(199, 37, 78); border-radius: 4px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(249, 242, 244);">.dropup</code><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; display: inline !important; float: none; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"> 类，可以让菜单向上弹出（默认是向下弹出的）</span></div><div style="box-sizing: border-box; overflow: auto; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace; font-size: 13px; display: block; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); border: 0px; border-radius: 4px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: transparent;"><code style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace; font-size: inherit; padding: 0px 45px 0px 0px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); border-radius: 0px; display: inline-block; background-color: transparent;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;div</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">class=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;dropup&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span><br/>
  <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;button</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">class=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;btn btn-default dropdown-toggle&quot;</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">type=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;button&quot;</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">id=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;dropdownMenu2&quot;</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">data-toggle=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;dropdown&quot;</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">aria-haspopup=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;true&quot;</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">aria-expanded=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;false&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span><br/>
    Dropup<br/>
    <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;span</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">class=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;caret&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;&lt;/span&gt;</span><br/>
  <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;/button&gt;</span><br/>
  <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;ul</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">class=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;dropdown-menu&quot;</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">aria-labelledby=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;dropdownMenu2&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span><br/>
    <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;li&gt;&lt;a</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">href=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;#&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span>Action<span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</span><br/>
    <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;li&gt;&lt;a</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">href=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;#&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span>Another action<span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</span><br/>
    <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;li&gt;&lt;a</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">href=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;#&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span>Something else here<span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</span><br/>
    <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;li&gt;&lt;a</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">href=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;#&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span>Separated link<span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</span></code><div><span style="font-size: inherit;"><span style="background-color: transparent;"> </span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);"><span style="background-color: transparent;"><span style="font-size: inherit;">&lt;/ul&gt;</span></span></span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: inherit;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);"><span style="background-color: transparent;"><span style="font-size: inherit;">&lt;/div&gt;</span></span></span></span></div></div><div><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif; font-weight: 500; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); margin-top: 20px; margin-bottom: 10px; font-size: 30px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">对齐</h2><div style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px 0px 1em; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><span style="font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif;">B默认情况下，下拉菜单自动沿着父元素的上沿和左侧被定位为 100% 宽度。 为 </span></span></span><code style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace; font-size: 14.4px; padding: 2px 4px; color: rgb(199, 37, 78); border-radius: 4px; background-color: rgb(249, 242, 244);">.dropdown-menu</code><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><span style="font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif;"> 添加 </span></span></span><code style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace; font-size: 14.4px; padding: 2px 4px; color: rgb(199, 37, 78); border-radius: 4px; background-color: rgb(249, 242, 244);">.dropdown-menu-right</code><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><span style="font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif;"> 类可以让菜单右对齐。</span></span></span></div><div><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><span style="font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif;"><br/></span></span></span></div><div style="box-sizing: border-box; overflow: auto; display: block; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); border: 0px; border-top-left-radius: 4px; border-top-right-radius: 4px; border-bottom-right-radius: 4px; border-bottom-left-radius: 4px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: transparent;"><code style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace; font-size: inherit; padding: 0px 45px 0px 0px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); border-radius: 0px; display: inline-block; background-color: transparent;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;ul</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">class=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;dropdown-menu dropdown-menu-right&quot;</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">aria-labelledby=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;dLabel&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span><br/>
  ...</code><div><span style="font-size: 13px;"><span style="font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);"><span style="background-color: transparent;"><span style="font-size: inherit;">&lt;/ul&gt;</span></span></span></span></span></div></div><div><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif; font-weight: 500; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); margin-top: 20px; margin-bottom: 10px; font-size: 30px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">标题</h2><div style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px 0px 1em; font-size: 16px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div>在任何下拉菜单中均可通过添加标题来标明一组动作。</div></div></div><div style="box-sizing: border-box; overflow: auto; display: block; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; border: 0px; border-top-left-radius: 4px; border-top-right-radius: 4px; border-bottom-right-radius: 4px; border-bottom-left-radius: 4px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: transparent;"><code style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace; font-size: inherit; padding: 0px 45px 0px 0px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); border-radius: 0px; display: inline-block; background-color: transparent;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;ul</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">class=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;dropdown-menu&quot;</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">aria-labelledby=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;dropdownMenu3&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span><br/>
  ...<br/>
  <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;li</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">class=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;dropdown-header&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span>Dropdown header<span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;/li&gt;</span><br/>
  ...</code><div><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><span style="font-size: 13px;"><span style="font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);"><span style="background-color: transparent;"><span style="font-size: inherit;">&lt;/ul&gt;</span></span></span></span></span></span></div><div><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><span style="font-size: 13px;"><span style="font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace;"><span style="color: rgb(47, 111, 159);"><br/></span></span></span></span></div><div><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><span style="font-size: 13px;"><span style="font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace;"><span style="color: rgb(47, 111, 159);"><br/></span></span></span></span></div><div><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif; font-weight: 500; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); margin-top: 20px; margin-bottom: 10px; font-size: 30px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">分割线</h2><div style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px 0px 1em; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><span style="font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif;">为下拉菜单添加一条分割线，用于将多个链接分组</span></span></span></div><div><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><span style="font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif;"><br/></span></span></span></div><div style="box-sizing: border-box; overflow: auto; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace; font-size: 13px; display: block; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); border: 0px; border-radius: 4px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: transparent;"><code style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace; font-size: inherit; padding: 0px 45px 0px 0px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); border-radius: 0px; display: inline-block; background-color: transparent;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;ul</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">class=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;dropdown-menu&quot;</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">aria-labelledby=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;dropdownMenuDivider&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span><br/>
  ...<br/>
  <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;li</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">role=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;separator&quot;</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">class=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;divider&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</span><br/>
  ...<br/><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;/ul&gt;</span></code></div><div><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif; font-weight: 500; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); margin-top: 20px; margin-bottom: 10px; font-size: 30px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">禁用的菜单项</h2><div style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px 0px 1em; font-size: 16px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div>为下拉菜单中的 <code style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace; font-size: 14.4px; padding: 2px 4px; color: rgb(199, 37, 78); border-radius: 4px; background-color: rgb(249, 242, 244);">&lt;li&gt;</code> 元素添加 <code style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace; font-size: 14.4px; padding: 2px 4px; color: rgb(199, 37, 78); border-radius: 4px; background-color: rgb(249, 242, 244);">.disabled</code> 类，从而禁用相应的菜单项。</div></div></div><div style="box-sizing: border-box; overflow: auto; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace; font-size: 13px; display: block; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); border: 0px; border-radius: 4px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: transparent;"><code style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace; font-size: inherit; padding: 0px 45px 0px 0px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); border-radius: 0px; display: inline-block; background-color: transparent;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;ul</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">class=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;dropdown-menu&quot;</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">aria-labelledby=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;dropdownMenu4&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span><br/>
  <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;li&gt;&lt;a</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">href=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;#&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span>Regular link<span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</span><br/>
  <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;li</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">class=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;disabled&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;&lt;a</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">href=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;#&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span>Disabled link<span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</span></code><div><span style="font-size: inherit;"><span style="background-color: transparent;"> </span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);"><span style="background-color: transparent;"><span style="font-size: inherit;">&lt;li&gt;&lt;a</span></span></span><span style="background-color: transparent;"><span style="font-size: inherit;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);"><span style="background-color: transparent;"><span style="font-size: inherit;">href=</span></span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);"><span style="background-color: transparent;"><span style="font-size: inherit;">&quot;#&quot;</span></span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);"><span style="background-color: transparent;"><span style="font-size: inherit;">&gt;</span></span></span><span style="background-color: transparent;"><span style="font-size: inherit;">Another link</span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);"><span style="background-color: transparent;"><span style="font-size: inherit;">&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</span></span></span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: inherit;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);"><span style="background-color: transparent;"><span style="font-size: inherit;">&lt;/ul&gt;</span></span></span></span></div></div><div><span style="font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><br/></span></span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><br/></span></span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><br/></span></span></span></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></span>

<a name="1236"/>
<h1>Well</h1>

<div>
<span><div><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif; font-weight: 500; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); margin-top: 20px; margin-bottom: 10px; font-size: 30px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">默认效果</h2><div style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px 0px 1em; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><span style="font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif;">把 Well 用在元素上，能有嵌入（inset）的的简单效果。</span></span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><br/></span></span></span></div><div><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><span style="font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif;"><br/></span></span></span></div><div style="box-sizing: border-box; <a name="1234"/>
<h1>具有响应式特性的嵌入内容</h1>
<div>
<table bgcolor="#D4DDE5" border="0">
<tr><td><b>创建时间：</b></td><td><i>2016-8-30 20:33</i></td></tr>
<tr><td><b>更新时间：</b></td><td><i>2016-8-30 20:35</i></td></tr>
<tr><td><b>作者：</b></td><td><i>李洪岩</i></td></tr>
</table>
</div>
<br/>

<div>
<span><div><p style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px 0px 1em; font-size: 16px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">根据被嵌入内容的外部容器的宽度，自动创建一个固定的比例，从而让浏览器自动确定视频或 slideshow 的尺寸，能够在各种设备上缩放。</p><p style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px 0px 1em; font-size: 16px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">这些规则被直接应用在 <code style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace; font-size: 14.4px; padding: 2px 4px; color: rgb(199, 37, 78); border-radius: 4px; background-color: rgb(249, 242, 244);">&lt;iframe&gt;</code>、<code style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace; font-size: 14.4px; padding: 2px 4px; color: rgb(199, 37, 78); border-radius: 4px; background-color: rgb(249, 242, 244);">&lt;embed&gt;</code>、<code style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace; font-size: 14.4px; padding: 2px 4px; color: rgb(199, 37, 78); border-radius: 4px; background-color: rgb(249, 242, 244);">&lt;video&gt;</code> 和 <code style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace; font-size: 14.4px; padding: 2px 4px; color: rgb(199, 37, 78); border-radius: 4px; background-color: rgb(249, 242, 244);">&lt;object&gt;</code> 元素上。如果你希望让最终样式与其他属性相匹配，还可以明确地使用一个派生出来的 <code style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace; font-size: 14.4px; padding: 2px 4px; color: rgb(199, 37, 78); border-radius: 4px; background-color: rgb(249, 242, 244);">.embed-responsive-item</code> 类。</p><div style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px 0px 1em; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><span style="font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box; font-weight: 700;">超级提示：</strong> 不需要为 </span></span></span><code style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace; font-size: 14.4px; padding: 2px 4px; color: rgb(199, 37, 78); border-radius: 4px; background-color: rgb(249, 242, 244);">&lt;iframe&gt;</code><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><span style="font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif;"> 元素设置 </span></span></span><code style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace; font-size: 14.4px; padding: 2px 4px; color: rgb(199, 37, 78); border-radius: 4px; background-color: rgb(249, 242, 244);">frameborder=&quot;0&quot;</code><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><span style="font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif;"> 属性，因为我们已经替你这样做了！</span></span></span></div><div><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><span style="font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif;"><br/></span></span></span></div><div style="box-sizing: border-box; overflow: auto; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace; font-size: 13px; display: block; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); border: 0px; border-radius: 4px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: transparent;"><div><span style="font-size: inherit;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(153, 153, 153);"><span style="background-color: transparent;">&lt;!-- 16:9 aspect ratio --&gt;</span></span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: inherit;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);"><span style="background-color: transparent;"><span style="font-size: inherit;">&lt;div</span></span></span><span style="background-color: transparent;"><span style="font-size: inherit;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);"><span style="background-color: transparent;"><span style="font-size: inherit;">&gt;</span></span></span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: inherit;"><span style="background-color: transparent;"> </span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);"><span style="background-color: transparent;"><span style="font-size: inherit;">&lt;iframe</span></span></span><span style="background-color: transparent;"><span style="font-size: inherit;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);"><span style="background-color: transparent;"><span style="font-size: inherit;">&gt;&lt;/iframe&gt;</span></span></span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: inherit;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);"><span style="background-color: transparent;"><span style="font-size: inherit;">&lt;/div&gt;</span></span></span></span></div><code style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace; font-size: inherit; padding: 0px 45px 0px 0px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); border-radius: 0px; display: inline-block; background-color: transparent;"><br/></code><div><span style="font-size: inherit;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(153, 153, 153);"><span style="background-color: transparent;">&lt;!-- 4:3 aspect ratio --&gt;</span></span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: inherit;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);"><span style="background-color: transparent;"><span style="font-size: inherit;">&lt;div</span></span></span><span style="background-color: transparent;"><span style="font-size: inherit;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);"><span style="background-color: transparent;"><span style="font-size: inherit;">class=</span></span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);"><span style="background-color: transparent;"><span style="font-size: inherit;">&quot;embed-responsive embed-responsive-4by3&quot;</span></span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);"><span style="background-color: transparent;"><span style="font-size: inherit;">&gt;</span></span></span></span></div><div><code style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace; font-size: inherit; padding: 0px 45px 0px 0px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); border-radius: 0px; display: inline-block; background-color: transparent;">  <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;iframe</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">class=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;embed-responsive-item&quot;</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">src=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;...&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;&lt;/iframe&gt;</span></code></div><div><code style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace; font-size: inherit; padding: 0px 45px 0px 0px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); border-radius: 0px; display: inline-block; background-color: transparent;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;/div&gt;</span></code></div></div></div></div></span>
</div>
<hr>
<a name="1232"/>
<h1>面板-- .panel</h1>
<div>
<table bgcolor="#D4DDE5" border="0">
<tr><td><b>创建时间：</b></td><td><i>2016-8-30 20:05</i></td></tr>
<tr><td><b>更新时间：</b></td><td><i>2016-8-30 20:29</i></td></tr>
<tr><td><b>作者：</b></td><td><i>李洪岩</i></td></tr>
</table>
</div>
<br/>

<div>
<span><div><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 300; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; display: inline !important; float: none; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">虽然不总是必须，但是某些时候你可能需要将某些 DOM 内容放到一个盒子里。对于这种情况，可以试试面板组件。</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif;"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><br/></span></span></span></span></div><div><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif; font-weight: 500; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); margin-top: 20px; margin-bottom: 10px; font-size: 30px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">基本实例</h2><div style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px 0px 1em; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><span style="font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif;">默认的 </span></span></span><code style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace; font-size: 14.4px; padding: 2px 4px; color: rgb(199, 37, 78); border-radius: 4px; background-color: rgb(249, 242, 244);">.panel</code><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><span style="font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif;"> 组件所做的只是设置基本的边框（border）和内补（padding）来包含内容。</span></span></span></div><div><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><span style="font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif;"><br/></span></span></span></div><div style="box-sizing: border-box; overflow: auto; display: block; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; border: 0px; border-top-left-radius: 4px; border-top-right-radius: 4px; border-bottom-right-radius: 4px; border-bottom-left-radius: 4px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: transparent;"><div style="box-sizing: border-box; position: relative; padding: 45px 15px 15px; margin: 0px 0px 15px; border: 1px solid rgb(221, 221, 221); box-shadow: none; border-radius: 4px 4px 0px 0px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-bottom: 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(221, 221, 221); border-radius: 4px; box-shadow: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.0470588) 0px 1px 1px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="box-sizing: border-box; padding: 15px;">Basic panel example</div></div></div><div style="box-sizing: border-box; position: relative; display: block; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; position: absolute; top: -16px; right: 0px; z-index: 10; display: block; padding: 5px 8px; font-size: 12px; color: rgb(118, 118, 118); cursor: pointer; border: 1px solid rgb(225, 225, 232); border-radius: 0px 0px 0px 4px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">复制</span></div><div style="box-sizing: border-box; padding: 9px 14px; margin: -16px 0px 15px; border: 1px solid rgb(225, 225, 232); border-radius: 0px 0px 4px 4px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 249);"><div style="box-sizing: border-box; overflow: auto; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace; font-size: 13px; display: block; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); border: 0px; border-radius: 4px; background-color: transparent;"><code style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace; font-size: inherit; padding: 0px 45px 0px 0px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); border-radius: 0px; display: inline-block; background-color: transparent;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;div</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">class=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;panel panel-default&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span><br/>
  <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;div</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">class=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;panel-body&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span><br/>
    Basic panel example</code><div><span style="font-size: inherit;"><span style="background-color: transparent;"> </span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);"><span style="background-color: transparent;"><span style="font-size: inherit;">&lt;/div&gt;</span></span></span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: inherit;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);"><span style="background-color: transparent;"><span style="font-size: inherit;">&lt;/div&gt;</span></span></span></span></div></div></div><div><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><span style="font-size: 13px;"><span style="font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace;"><span style="color: rgb(47, 111, 159);"><br/></span></span></span></span></div><div><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif; font-weight: 500; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); margin-top: 20px; margin-bottom: 10px; font-size: 30px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">带标题的面版</h2><p style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px 0px 1em; font-size: 16px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">通过 <code style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace; font-size: 14.4px; padding: 2px 4px; color: rgb(199, 37, 78); border-radius: 4px; background-color: rgb(249, 242, 244);">.panel-heading</code> 可以很简单地为面板加入一个标题容器。你也可以通过添加设置了 <code style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace; font-size: 14.4px; padding: 2px 4px; color: rgb(199, 37, 78); border-radius: 4px; background-color: rgb(249, 242, 244);">.panel-title</code> 类的 <code style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace; font-size: 14.4px; padding: 2px 4px; color: rgb(199, 37, 78); border-radius: 4px; background-color: rgb(249, 242, 244);">&lt;h1&gt;</code>-<code style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace; font-size: 14.4px; padding: 2px 4px; color: rgb(199, 37, 78); border-radius: 4px; background-color: rgb(249, 242, 244);">&lt;h6&gt;</code> 标签，添加一个预定义样式的标题。</p><div style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px 0px 1em; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><span style="font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif;">为了给链接设置合适的颜色，务必将链接放到带有 </span></span></span><code style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace; font-size: 14.4px; padding: 2px 4px; color: rgb(199, 37, 78); border-radius: 4px; background-color: rgb(249, 242, 244);">.panel-title</code><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><span style="font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif;"> 类的标题标签内。</span></span></span></div><div><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><span style="font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif;"><br/></span></span></span></div><div style="box-sizing: border-box; position: relative; padding: 45px 15px 15px; margin: 0px 0px 15px; border: 1px solid rgb(221, 221, 221); box-shadow: none; border-radius: 4px 4px 0px 0px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-bottom: 20px; border: 1px solid rgb(221, 221, 221); border-radius: 4px; box-shadow: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.0470588) 0px 1px 1px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="box-sizing: border-box; padding: 10px 15px; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-color: rgb(221, 221, 221); border-top-left-radius: 3px; border-top-right-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); background-color: rgb(245, 245, 245);">Panel heading without title</div><div style="box-sizing: border-box; padding: 15px;">Panel content</div></div><div style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-bottom: 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(221, 221, 221); border-radius: 4px; box-shadow: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.0470588) 0px 1px 1px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="box-sizing: border-box; padding: 10px 15px; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: solid; border-color: rgb(221, 221, 221); border-top-left-radius: 3px; border-top-right-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); background-color: rgb(245, 245, 245);"><h3 style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: inherit; font-weight: 500; color: inherit; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-size: 16px;">Panel title</h3></div><div style="box-sizing: border-box; padding: 15px;">Panel content</div></div></div><div style="box-sizing: border-box; position: relative; display: block; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; position: absolute; top: -16px; right: 0px; z-index: 10; display: block; padding: 5px 8px; font-size: 12px; color: rgb(118, 118, 118); cursor: pointer; border: 1px solid rgb(225, 225, 232); border-radius: 0px 0px 0px 4px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">复制</span></div><div style="box-sizing: border-box; padding: 9px 14px; margin: -16px 0px 15px; border: 1px solid rgb(225, 225, 232); border-radius: 0px 0px 4px 4px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 249);"><div style="box-sizing: border-box; overflow: auto; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace; font-size: 13px; display: block; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); border: 0px; border-radius: 4px; background-color: transparent;"><code style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace; font-size: inherit; padding: 0px 45px 0px 0px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); border-radius: 0px; display: inline-block; background-color: transparent;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;div</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box;   <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;div</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">class=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;panel-heading&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span>Panel heading without title<span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;/div&gt;</span><br/>
  <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;div</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">class=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;panel-body&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span><br/>
    Panel content<br/>
  <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;/div&gt;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;/div&gt;</span><br/><br/><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;div</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">class=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;panel panel-default&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span><br/>
  <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;div</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">class=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;panel-heading&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span><br/>
    <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;h3</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">class=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;panel-title&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span>Panel title<span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;/h3&gt;</span><br/>
  <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;/div&gt;</span><br/>
  <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;div</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">class=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;panel-body&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span><br/>
    Panel content</code><div><span style="font-size: inherit;"><span style="background-color: transparent;"> </span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);"><span style="background-color: transparent;"><span style="font-size: inherit;">&lt;/div&gt;</span></span></span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: inherit;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);"><span style="background-color: transparent;"><span style="font-size: inherit;">&lt;/div&gt;</span></span></span></span></div></div></div></div></div><div><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><span style="font-size: 13px;"><span style="font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace;"><span style="color: rgb(47, 111, 159);"><br/></span></span></span></span></div><div><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif; font-weight: 500; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); margin-top: 20px; margin-bottom: 10px; font-size: 30px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">带脚注的面版</h2><div style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px 0px 1em; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><span style="font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif;">把按钮或次要的文本放入 </span></span></span><code style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace; font-size: 14.4px; padding: 2px 4px; color: rgb(199, 37, 78); border-radius: 4px; background-color: rgb(249, 242, 244);">.panel-footer</code><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><span style="font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif;"> 容器内。注意面版的脚注<strong style="box-sizing: border-box; font-weight: 700;">不会</strong>从情境效果中继承颜色，因为他们并不是主要内容。</span></span></span></div><div><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><span style="font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif;"><br/></span></span></span></div><div style="box-sizing: border-box;
