  <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;div</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">class=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;panel-heading&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span>Panel heading<span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;/div&gt;</span><br/>
  <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;div</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">class=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;panel-body&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span><br/>
    <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;p&gt;</span>...<span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;/p&gt;</span><br/>
  <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;/div&gt;</span><br/><br/>
  <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(153, 153, 153);">&lt;!-- List group --&gt;</span><br/>
  <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;ul</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">class=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;list-group&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span><br/>
    <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;li</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">class=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;list-group-item&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span>Cras justo odio<span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;/li&gt;</span><br/>
    <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;li</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">class=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;list-group-item&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span>Dapibus ac facilisis in<span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;/li&gt;</span><br/>
    <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;li</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">class=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;list-group-item&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span>Morbi leo risus<span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;/li&gt;</span><br/>
    <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;li</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">class=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;list-group-item&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span>Porta ac consectetur ac<span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;/li&gt;</span><br/>
    <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;li</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">class=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;list-group-item&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span>Vestibulum at eros<span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;/li&gt;</span></code><div><span style="font-size: inherit;"><span style="background-color: transparent;"> </span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);"><span style="background-color: transparent;"><span style="font-size: inherit;">&lt;/ul&gt;</span></span></span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: inherit;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);"><span style="background-color: transparent;"><span style="font-size: inherit;">&lt;/div&gt;</span></span></span></span></div></div></div></div><div><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><span style="font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif;"><br/></span></span></span></div></div></div><div><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><span style="font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif;"><br/></span></span></span></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></span>
</div>
<hr>
<a name="1230"/>
<h1>列表组--list-group</h1>
<div>
<table bgcolor="#D4DDE5" border="0">
<tr><td><b>创建时间：</b></td><td><i>2016-8-30 19:27</i></td></tr>
<tr><td><b>更新时间：</b></td><td><i>2016-8-30 20:06</i></td></tr>
<tr><td><b>作者：</b></td><td><i>李洪岩</i></td></tr>
</table>
</div>
<br/>

<div>
<span><div><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 300; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; display: inline !important; float: none; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">列表组是灵活又强大的组件，不仅能用于显示一组简单的元素，还能用于复杂的定制的内容</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif;"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><br/></span></span></span></span></div><div><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif; font-weight: 500; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); margin-top: 20px; margin-bottom: 10px; font-size: 30px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">基本实例</h2><div style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px 0px 1em; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><span style="font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif;">最简单的列表组仅仅是一个带有多个列表条目的无序列表，另外还需要设置适当的类。我们提供了一些预定义的样式，你可以根据自身的需求通过 CSS 自己定制</span></span></span></div><div style="box-sizing: border-box; overflow: auto; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace; font-size: 13px; display: block; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); border: 0px; border-radius: 4px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: transparent;"><code style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace; font-size: inherit; padding: 0px 45px 0px 0px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); border-radius: 0px; display: inline-block; background-color: transparent;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;ul</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">class=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;list-group&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span><br/>
  <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;li</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">class=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;list-group-item&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span>Cras justo odio<span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;/li&gt;</span><br/>
  <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;li</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">class=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;list-group-item&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span>Dapibus ac facilisis in<span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;/li&gt;</span><br/>
  <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;li</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">class=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;list-group-item&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span>Morbi leo risus<span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;/li&gt;</span><br/>
  <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;li</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">class=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;list-group-item&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span>Porta ac consectetur ac<span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;/li&gt;</span></code><div><span style="font-size: inherit;"><span style="background-color: transparent;"> </span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);"><span style="background-color: transparent;"><span style="font-size: inherit;">&lt;li</span></span></span><span style="background-color: transparent;"><span style="font-size: inherit;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);"><span style="background-color: transparent;"><span style="font-size: inherit;">class=</span></span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);"><span style="background-color: transparent;"><span style="font-size: inherit;">&quot;list-group-item&quot;</span></span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);"><span style="background-color: transparent;"><span style="font-size: inherit;">&gt;</span></span></span><span style="background-color: transparent;"><span style="font-size: inherit;">Vestibulum at eros</span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);"><span style="background-color: transparent;"><span style="font-size: inherit;">&lt;/li&gt;</span></span></span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: inherit;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);"><span style="background-color: transparent;"><span style="font-size: inherit;">&lt;/ul&gt;</span></span></span></span></div></div><div><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><span style="font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif;"><br/></span></span></span></div><div><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif; font-weight: 500; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); margin-top: 20px; margin-bottom: 10px; font-size: 30px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">徽章</h2><div style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px 0px 1em; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><span style="font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif;">给列表组加入徽章组件，它会自动被放在右边。</span></span></span></div><div style="box-sizing: border-box; overflow: auto; display: block; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; border: 0px; border-top-left-radius: 4px; border-top-right-radius: 4px; border-bottom-right-radius: 4px; border-bottom-left-radius: 4px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: transparent;"><code style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace; font-size: inherit; padding: 0px 45px 0px 0px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); border-radius: 0px; display: inline-block; background-color: transparent;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;ul</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">class=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;list-group&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span><br/>
  <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;li</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">class=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;list-group-item&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span><br/>
    <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;span</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">class=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;badge&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span>14<span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;/span&gt;</span><br/>
    Cras justo odio</code><div><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><span style="font-size: 13px;"><span style="font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace;"><span style="font-size: inherit;"><span style="background-color: transparent;"> </span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);"><span style="background-color: transparent;"><span style="font-size: inherit;">&lt;/li&gt;</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></div><div><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><span style="font-size: 13px;"><span style="font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace;"><span style="font-size: inherit;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);"><span style="background-color: transparent;"><span style="font-size: inherit;">&lt;/ul&gt;</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></div><div><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><span style="font-size: 13px;"><span style="font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace;"><span style="color: rgb(47, 111, 159);"><br/></span></span></span></span></div><div><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif; font-weight: 500; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); margin-top: 20px; margin-bottom: 10px; font-size: 30px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">链接</h2><div style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px 0px 1em; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><span style="font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif;">用 </span></span></span><code style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace; font-size: 14.4px; padding: 2px 4px; color: rgb(199, 37, 78); border-radius: 4px; background-color: rgb(249, 242, 244);">&lt;a&gt;</code><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><span style="font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif;"> 标签代替 </span></span></span><code style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace; font-size: 14.4px; padding: 2px 4px; color: rgb(199, 37, 78); border-radius: 4px; background-color: rgb(249, 242, 244);">&lt;li&gt;</code><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><span style="font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif;"> 标签可以组成一个全部是链接的列表组（还要注意的是，我们需要将 </span></span></span><code style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace; font-size: 14.4px; padding: 2px 4px; color: rgb(199, 37, 78); border-radius: 4px; background-color: rgb(249, 242, 244);">&lt;ul&gt;</code><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><span style="font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif;"> 标签替换为 </span></span></span><code style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace; font-size: 14.4px; padding: 2px 4px; color: rgb(199, 37, 78); border-radius: 4px; background-color: rgb(249, 242, 244);">&lt;div&gt;</code><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><span style="font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif;">标签）。没必要给列表组中的每个元素都加一个父元素。</span></span></span></div><div><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><span style="font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif;"><br/></span></span></span></div><div style="box-sizing: border-box; overflow: auto; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace; font-size: 13px; display: block; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); border: 0px; border-radius: 4px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: transparent;"><code style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace; font-size: inherit; padding: 0px 45px 0px 0px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); border-radius: 0px; display: inline-block; background-color: transparent;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;div</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">class=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;list-group&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span><br/>
  <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;a</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">href=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;#&quot;</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">class=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;list-group-item active&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span><br/>
    Cras justo odio<br/>
  <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;/a&gt;</span><br/>
  <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;a</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">href=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;#&quot;</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">class=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;list-group-item&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span>Dapibus ac facilisis in<span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;/a&gt;</span><br/>
  <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;a</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">href=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;#&quot;</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">class=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;list-group-item&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span>Morbi leo risus<span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;/a&gt;</span><br/>
  <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;a</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">href=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;#&quot;</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box;   <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;li</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">class=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;list-group-item list-group-item-warning&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;   <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;a</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">href=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;#&quot;</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">定制内容</h2><div style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px 0px 1em; font-size: 16px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div>列表组中的每个元素都可以是任何 HTML 内容，甚至是像下面的带链接的列表组。</div><div><br/></div><div><br/></div></div></div></div></div><div><span style="font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><br/></span></span></span></div><div><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><span style="font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif;"><br/></span></span></span></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></span>

<a name="1228"/>
<h1>媒体对象</h1>
<div>
<table bgcolor="#D4DDE5" border="0">
<tr><td><b>创建时间：</b></td><td><i>2016-8-30 17:14</i></td></tr>

</div>

<div>
<span><div> 
<h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif; font-weight: 500; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); margin-top: 20px; margin-bottom: 10px; font-size: 30px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">默认样式</h2><div style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px 0px 1em; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><span style="font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif;">默认样式的媒体对象组件允许在一个内容块的左边或右边展示一个多媒体内容（图像、视频、音频）。</span></span></span></div><div><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><span style="font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif;"><br/></span></span></span></div><div style="box-sizing: border-box; overflow: auto; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace; font-size: 13px; display: block; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); border: 0px; border-radius: 4px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: transparent;"><code style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace; font-size: inherit; padding: 0px 45px 0px 0px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); border-radius: 0px; display: inline-block; background-color: transparent;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;div</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">class=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;   <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;div</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">class=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;media-left&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span><br/>
    <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;a</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">href=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;#&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span><br/>
      <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;img</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">class=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;media-object&quot;</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">src=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;...&quot;</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">alt=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;...&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span><br/>
    <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;/a&gt;</span><br/>

    <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;h4</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">class=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;media-heading&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span>Media heading<span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;/h4&gt;</span><br/>
    ...</code><div><span style="font-size: inherit;"><span style="background-color: transparent;"> </span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);"><span style="background-color: transparent;"><span style="font-size: inherit;">&lt;/div&gt;</span></span></span></span></div><div><span style="color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">  &lt;div class=&quot;media-right&quot;&gt;</span></div><div><span style="color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">     &lt;a href=&quot;#&quot;&gt;</span></div><div><span style="color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">          &lt;img src=&quot;&quot;       <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;img</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">class=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;media-object&quot;</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">src=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;...&quot;</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">alt=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;...&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span><br/>

color: rgb(47, 111, 159);"><span style="font-size: inherit;">&lt;/a&gt;</span></span></span></span></code></div><div><span style="font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace;"><span style="font-size: inherit;"><span style="font-size: inherit;"><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><span style="background-color: transparent;"> </span></span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);"><span style="font-size: inherit;"><span style="background-color: transparent;">&lt;/div&gt;</span></span></span></span></span></span></div><div><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><span style="font-size: 13px;"><span style="font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace;"><span style="font-size: inherit;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);"><span style="background-color: transparent;"><span style="font-size: inherit;">&lt;/div&gt;</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></div><div><span style="font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace;"><span style="color: rgb(47, 111, 159);"><br/></span></span></div><div><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif; font-weight: 500; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); margin-top: 20px; margin-bottom: 10px; font-size: 30px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">媒体对象列表</h2><div style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px 0px 1em; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><span style="font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif;">用一点点额外的标记，就能在列表内使用媒体对象组件（对评论或文章列表很有用）</span></span></span></div><div style="box-sizing: border-box; overflow: auto; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace; font-size: 13px; display: block; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); border: 0px; border-radius: 4px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: transparent;"><code style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace; font-size: inherit; padding: 0px 45px 0px 0px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); border-radius: 0px; display: inline-block; background-color: transparent;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;ul</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">class=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;media-list&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span><br/>
  <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;li</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">class=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;media&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span><br/>
    <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;div</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">class=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;media-left&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span><br/>
      <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;a</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">href=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;#&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span><br/>
        <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;img</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">class=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;media-object&quot;</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">src=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;...&quot;</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">alt=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;...&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span><br/>
      <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;/a&gt;</span><br/>
    <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;/div&gt;</span><br/>
    <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;div</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">class=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;media-body&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span><br/>
      <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;h4</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">class=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;media-heading&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span>Media heading<span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;/h4&gt;</span><br/>
      ...<br/>
    <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;/div&gt;</span></code><div><span style="font-size: inherit;"><span style="background-color: transparent;"> </span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);"><span style="background-color: transparent;"><span style="font-size: inherit;">&lt;/li&gt;</span></span></span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: inherit;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);"><span style="background-color: transparent;"><span style="font-size: inherit;">&lt;/ul&gt;</span></span></span></span></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></span>

<a name="1226"/>
<h1>进度条--progress</h1>
<div>
<table bgcolor="#D4DDE5" border="0">
<tr><td><b>创建时间：</b></td><td><i>2016-8-30 16:42</i></td></tr>

background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">带有提示标签的进度条</h2><div style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px 0px 1em; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace; font-size: 14.4px; padding: 2px 4px; color: rgb(199, 37, 78); border-radius: 4px; background-color: rgb(249, 242, 244);">.sr-only</code><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><span style="font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif;"> 类的 </span></span></span><code style="box-sizing: border-box;     60%</code><div><span style="font-size: inherit;"><span style="background-color: transparent;"> </span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);"><span style="background-color: transparent;"><span style="font-size: inherit;">&lt;/div&gt;</span></span></span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: inherit;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; display: inline !important; float: none; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">在展示很低的百分比时，如果需要让文本提示能够清晰可见，可以为进度条设置 </span><code style="box-sizing: border-box; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div>为 <code style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace; font-size: 14.4px; padding: 2px 4px; <h1>警告框-- .alert alert-warning</h1>

color: rgb(79, 159, 207);"><span style="background-color: transparent;"><span style="font-size: inherit;">role=</span></span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);"><span style="background-color: transparent;"><span style="font-size: inherit;">&quot;alert&quot;</span></span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; <span><div><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif; font-weight: 500; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);   <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;div</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">class=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;col-xs-6 col-md-3&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span><br/>

      <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;img</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">src=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;...&quot;</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">alt=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;...&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span><br/>
    <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;/a&gt;</span></code><div><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><span style="font-size: 13px;"><span style="font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace;"><span style="font-size: inherit;"><span style="background-color: transparent;"> </span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif; font-weight: 500; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); margin-top: 20px; margin-bottom: 10px; font-size: 30px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">自定义内容</h2><div style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px 0px 1em; font-size: 16px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div>添加一点点额外的标签，就可以把任何类型的 HTML 内容，例如标题、段落或按钮，加入缩略图组件内。</div></div></div><div style="box-sizing: border-box; overflow: auto; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: transparent;"><code style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace; font-size: inherit; padding: 0px 45px 0px 0px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); border-radius: 0px; display: inline-block; background-color: transparent;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span><br/>
  <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;div</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">class=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;col-sm-6 col-md-4&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span><br/>
    <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;div</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">class=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;thumbnail&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span><br/>
      <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;img</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">src=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;...&quot;</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">alt=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;...&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span><br/>
      <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;div</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">class=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;caption&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span><br/>
        <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;h3&gt;</span>Thumbnail label<span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;/h3&gt;</span><br/>
        <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;p&gt;</span>...<span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;/p&gt;</span><br/>
        <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;p&gt;&lt;a</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">href=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;#&quot;</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">class=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;btn btn-primary&quot;</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">role=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;button&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span>Button<span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;/a&gt;</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;a</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">href=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;#&quot;</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">class=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;btn btn-default&quot;</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">role=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;button&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span>Button<span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</span><br/>
      <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;/div&gt;</span><br/>
    <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;/div&gt;</span></code><div><span style="font-size: inherit;"><span style="background-color: transparent;"> </span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);"><span style="background-color: transparent;"><span style="font-size: inherit;">&lt;/div&gt;</span></span></span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: inherit;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);"><span style="background-color: transparent;"><span style="font-size: inherit;">&lt;/div&gt;</span></span></span></span></div></div></div></div></div></span>

<a name="1220"/>
<h1>页头-- .page-header</h1>
<div>
<table bgcolor="#D4DDE5" border="0">
<tr><td><b>创建时间：</b></td><td><i>2016-8-30 15:51</i></td></tr>
<tr><td><b>更新时间：</b></td><td><i>2016-8-30 15:52</i></td></tr>
<tr><td><b>作者：</b></td><td><i>李洪岩</i></td></tr>
</table>
</div>
<br/>

<div>
<span><div><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; display: inline !important; float: none; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">页头组件能够为 </span><code style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace; font-size: 14.4px; padding: 2px 4px; color: rgb(199, 37, 78); border-radius: 4px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(249, 242, 244);">h1</code><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; display: inline !important; float: none; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"> 标签增加适当的空间，并且与页面的其他部分形成一定的分隔。它支持 </span><code style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace; font-size: 14.4px; padding: 2px 4px; color: rgb(199, 37, 78); border-radius: 4px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(249, 242, 244);">h1</code><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; display: inline !important; float: none; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"> 标签内内嵌 </span><code style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace; font-size: 14.4px; padding: 2px 4px; color: rgb(199, 37, 78); border-radius: 4px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(249, 242, 244);">small</code><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; display: inline !important; float: none; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"> 元素的默认效果，还支持大部分其他组件（需要增加一些额外的样式）。</span></div><div style="box-sizing: border-box; overflow: auto; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace; font-size: 13px; display: block; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); border: 0px; border-radius: 4px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: transparent;"><code style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace; font-size: inherit; padding: 0px 45px 0px 0px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); border-radius: 0px; display: inline-block; background-color: transparent;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;div</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">class=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;page-header&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span></code><div><span style="font-size: inherit;"><span style="background-color: transparent;"> </span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);"><span style="background-color: transparent;"><span style="font-size: inherit;">&lt;h1&gt;</span></span></span><span style="background-color: transparent;"><span style="font-size: inherit;">Example page header </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);"><span style="background-color: transparent;"><span style="font-size: inherit;">&lt;small&gt;</span></span></span><span style="background-color: transparent;"><span style="font-size: inherit;">Subtext for header</span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);"><span style="background-color: transparent;"><span style="font-size: inherit;">&lt;/small&gt;&lt;/h1&gt;</span></span></span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: inherit;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);"><span style="background-color: transparent;"><span style="font-size: inherit;">&lt;/div&gt;</span></span></span></span></div></div></span>
</div>

<a name="1208"/>
<h1>导航条-- .nav</h1>
<div>
<table bgcolor="#D4DDE5" border="0">
<tr><td><b>创建时间：</b></td><td><i>2016-8-30 14:26</i></td></tr>

font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace; font-size: 14.4px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; display: inline !important; float: none; background-color: rgb(249, 242, 244);">.navbar-fixed-bottom</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14px;">当使用</span><span style="color: rgb(199, 37, 78); overflow: auto; font-size: 13px; display: block; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; border: 0px; border-top-left-radius: 4px; border-top-right-radius: 4px; border-bottom-right-radius: 4px; border-bottom-left-radius: 4px; margin-bottom: 0px;">}</span></code></div></div><div><span style="font-size: 14px;"><br/></span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14px;">静止在顶部</span></div><div><span style="color: rgb(199, 37, 78); font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace;     <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;li</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">class=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;previous&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;&lt;a</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">href=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;#&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;&lt;span</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">aria-hidden=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;true&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(153, 153, 153);">&amp;larr;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;/span&gt;</span> Older<span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</span><br/>
    <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;li</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">class=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;next&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;&lt;a</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">href=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;#&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span>Newer <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;span</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">aria-hidden=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;true&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(153, 153, 153);">&amp;rarr;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</span></code><div><span style="font-size: inherit;"><span style="background-color: transparent;"> </span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);"><span style="background-color: transparent;"><span style="font-size: inherit;">&lt;/ul&gt;</span></span></span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: inherit;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);"><span style="background-color: transparent;"><span style="font-size: inherit;">&lt;/nav&gt;</span></span></span></span></div></div><div style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><span style="font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace;"><span style="font-size: 13px;"><span style="color: rgb(47, 111, 159);"><br/></span></span></span></div></div></div></span>

<h1>徽章-.badge</h1>
<div>
<table bgcolor="#D4DDE5" border="0">

<br/>

<div>
<span><div><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 300; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; display: inline !important; float: none; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">给链接、导航等元素嵌套 </span><code style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace; font-size: 14.4px; padding: 2px 4px; color: rgb(199, 37, 78); border-radius: 4px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 300; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(249, 242, 244);">&lt;span class=&quot;badge&quot;&gt;</code><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 300; letter-spacing: normal; font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; <h1>巨幕--.jumbotron</h1>
<div>
<table bgcolor="#D4DDE5" border="0">
<tr><td><b>创建时间：</b></td><td><i>2016-8-30 15:43</i></td></tr>
<tr><td><b>更新时间：</b></td><td><i>2016-8-30 15:47</i></td></tr>
<tr><td><b>作者：</b></td><td><i>李洪岩</i></td></tr>
</table>

<br/>

<div>
<span><div><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; display: inline !important; float: none; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">这是一个轻量、灵活的组件，它能延伸至整个浏览器视口来展示网站上的关键内容</span></div><div style="box-sizing: border-box; overflow: auto; display: block; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; border: 0px; border-top-left-radius: 4px; border-top-right-radius: 4px; border-bottom-right-radius: 4px; border-bottom-left-radius: 4px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: transparent;"><code style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace; font-size: inherit; padding: 0px 45px 0px 0px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); border-radius: 0px; display: inline-block; background-color: transparent;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;div</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">class=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;jumbotron&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span><br/>
  <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;h1&gt;</span>Hello, world!<span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;/h1&gt;</span><br/>
  <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;p&gt;</span>...<span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;/p&gt;</span></code><div><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><span style="font-size: 13px;"><span style="font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace;"><span style="font-size: inherit;"><span style="background-color: transparent;"> </span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);"><span style="background-color: transparent;"><span style="font-size: inherit;">&lt;p&gt;&lt;a</span></span></span><span style="background-color: transparent;"><span style="font-size: inherit;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);"><span style="background-color: transparent;"><span style="font-size: inherit;">class=</span></span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);"><span style="background-color: transparent;"><span style="font-size: inherit;">&quot;btn btn-primary btn-lg&quot;</span></span></span><span style="background-color: transparent;"><span style="font-size: inherit;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);"><span style="background-color: transparent;"><span style="font-size: inherit;">href=</span></span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);"><span style="background-color: transparent;"><span style="font-size: inherit;">&quot;#&quot;</span></span></span><span style="background-color: transparent;"><span style="font-size: inherit;"> </span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);"><span style="background-color: transparent;"><span style="font-size: inherit;">role=</span></span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);"><span style="background-color: transparent;"><span style="font-size: inherit;">&quot;button&quot;</span></span></span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);"><span style="background-color: transparent;"><span style="font-size: inherit;">&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></div><div><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><span style="font-size: 13px;"><span style="font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace;"><span style="font-size: inherit;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;   <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;div</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">class=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;container&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span><br/>
    ...</code><div><span style="font-size: inherit;"><span style="background-color: transparent;"> </span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);"><span style="background-color: transparent;"><span style="font-size: inherit;">&lt;/div&gt;</span></span></span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: inherit;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);"><span style="background-color: transparent;"><span style="font-size: inherit;">&lt;/div&gt;</span></span></span></span></div></div></div></span>

<span><div>实例</div><div style="box-sizing: border-box; overflow: auto; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace; font-size: 13px; display: block; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(51, 122, 183);">Primary</span><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; display: inline !important; float: none; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"> </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; display: inline; padding: 0.2em 0.6em 0.3em; font-size: 12px; font-weight: 700; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); text-align: center; white-space: nowrap; vertical-align: baseline; border-radius: 0.25em; font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(92, 184, 92);">Success</span><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; display: inline !important; float: none; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"> </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; display: inline; padding: 0.2em 0.6em 0.3em; font-size: 12px; font-weight: 700; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); text-align: center; white-space: nowrap; vertical-align: baseline; border-radius: 0.25em; font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(91, 192, 222);">Info</span><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; display: inline !important; float: none; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"> </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; display: inline; padding: 0.2em 0.6em 0.3em; font-size: 12px; font-weight: 700; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); text-align: center; white-space: nowrap; vertical-align: baseline; border-radius: 0.25em; font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(240, 173, 78);">Warning</span><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; display: inline !important; float: none; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"> </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; display: inline; padding: 0.2em 0.6em 0.3em; font-size: 12px; font-weight: 700; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); text-align: center; white-space: nowrap; vertical-align: baseline; border-radius: 0.25em; font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(217, 83, 79);">Danger</span></div><div style="box-sizing: border-box; overflow: auto; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace; font-size: 13px; display: block; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); border: 0px; border-radius: 4px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: transparent;"><div><span style="color: rgb(47, 111, 159);"><br/></span></div><div><code style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace; font-size: inherit; padding: 0px 45px 0px 0px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); border-radius: 0px; display: inline-block; background-color: transparent;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;span</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">class=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;label label-default&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span>Default<span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;/span&gt;</span></code></div><div><code style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace; font-size: inherit; padding: 0px 45px 0px 0px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); border-radius: 0px; display: inline-block; background-color: transparent;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;span</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">class=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;label label-primary&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span>Primary<span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;/span&gt;</span></code></div><div><code style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace; font-size: inherit; padding: 0px 45px 0px 0px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); border-radius: 0px; display: inline-block; background-color: transparent;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;span</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">class=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;label label-success&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span>Success<span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;/span&gt;</span></code></div><div><code style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace; font-size: inherit; padding: 0px 45px 0px 0px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); border-radius: 0px; display: inline-block; background-color: transparent;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;span</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">class=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;label label-info&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span>Info<span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;/span&gt;</span></code></div><div><code style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace; font-size: inherit; padding: 0px 45px 0px 0px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); border-radius: 0px; display: inline-block; background-color: transparent;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;span</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">class=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;label label-warning&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span>Warning<span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;/span&gt;</span></code></div><div><code style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace; font-size: inherit; padding: 0px 45px 0px 0px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); border-radius: 0px; display: inline-block; background-color: transparent;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;span</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(79, 159, 207);">class=</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(212, 73, 80);">&quot;label label-danger&quot;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&gt;</span>Danger<span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(47, 111, 159);">&lt;/span&gt;</span></code></div></div><div><br/></div><div><br/></div><div><h4 style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif; font-weight: 500; color: rgb(27, 128, 158); margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 5px; font-size: 18px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">如果标签数量很多怎么办？</h4><div style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; font-size: 16px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Microsoft Yahei', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'WenQuanYi Micro Hei', sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 1; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div>如果你有大量的设置为 <code style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace; font-size: 14.4px; padding: 2px 4px; color: rgb(199, 37, 78); border-radius: 3px; background-color: rgb(249, 242, 244);">inline</code> 属性的标签全部放在一个较窄的容器元素内，在页面上展示这些标签就会出现问题，每个标签就会有自己的一个 <code style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace; font-size: 14.4px; padding: 2px 4px; color: rgb(199, 37, 78); border-radius: 3px; background-color: rgb(249, 242, 244);">inline-block</code> 元素（就像图标一样）。解决的办法是为每个标签都设置为<code style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace; font-size: 14.4px; padding: 2px 4px; color: rgb(199, 37, 78); border-radius: 3px; background-color: rgb(249, 242, 244);">display: inline-block;</code> 属性。关于这个问题以及实例，请参考 <a href="https://github.com/twbs/bootstrap/issues/13219" style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 122, 183); text-decoration: none; margin-bottom: 0px; background-color: transparent;">#13219</a> 。</div></div></div></span>
</div>
<hr>

<h1>基本框架</h1>
